## TOPIC 01751: DAQmx_CI_CtrTimebase_DigFltr_TimebaseRate

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__general__properties__counter__timebase__digital__filter__timebase_1gaa82d02499d0f2bab14557b0b895ca030.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__general__properties__counter__timebase__digital__filter__timebase_1gaa82d02499d0f2bab14557b0b895ca030.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CI_CtrTimebase_DigFltr_TimebaseRateRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies in hertz the rate of the pulse width filter timebase. NI-DAQmx uses this value to compute settings for the filter.You can get/set/reset this property using:DAQmxGetCICtrTimebaseDigFltrTimebaseRateD

### DAQmx_CI_CtrTimebase_DigFltr_TimebaseRate

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_CtrTimebase_DigFltr_TimebaseRate

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies in hertz the rate of the pulse width filter timebase. NI-DAQmx uses this value to compute settings for the filter. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCICtrTimebaseDigFltrTimebaseRate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga04d49dbeebead28b51bb2480232bc0ff.html)
- [DAQmxSetCICtrTimebaseDigFltrTimebaseRate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga8d98f2d4f586a776ffd35bbfe5934396.html)
- [DAQmxResetCICtrTimebaseDigFltrTimebaseRate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gad8bbb5b30fdaaaa33f9bfbe9ae4417e5.html)

### DAQmx_CI_FilterDelay

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_FilterDelay

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Indicates the amount of time between when the input signal transitions and when the filtered sample is read by the host device. This value is in the units specified with Filter Delay Units. | Not Settable |

You can get this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIFilterDelay](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga5818b04e3c9277723bf1b6ab4067a2a1.html)

### DAQmx_CI_Filter_Response

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_Filter_Response

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the corresponding filter response and defines the shape of the filter response. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_Comb | 16152 | Comb filter response. |
| DAQmx_Val_Bessel | 16153 | Bessel filter response. |
| DAQmx_Val_Brickwall | 16155 | Brickwall filter response. |
| DAQmx_Val_Butterworth | 16076 | Butterworth filter response. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIFilterResponse](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga939ead06e4d0035054c120acad477230.html)

- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CI_ThreshVoltageRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies the digital threshold value in Volts for high and low input transitions. Some devices do not support this for differential channels.You can get/set/reset this property using:DAQmxGetCIThreshVoltageDAQmxSetCIThreshVol

### DAQmx_CI_ThreshVoltage

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_ThreshVoltage

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the digital threshold value in Volts for high and low input transitions. Some devices do not support this for differential channels. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIThreshVoltage](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga35b6b9bd06d9d7c79a4fc1df8bee131b.html)

## TOPIC 01774: DAQmx_CI_MemMapEnable

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__general__properties__more__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga4eaa849c82b657327f18caf1bc750500.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__general__properties__more__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga4eaa849c82b657327f18caf1bc750500.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CI_MemMapEnableRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space

### DAQmx_CI_MemMapEnable

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_MemMapEnable

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIMemMapEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gae4870ed4a4f0295a530493477cc07c89.html)
- [DAQmxSetCIMemMapEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga68b6f9618b75c216bf24eca5d2af92e1.html)
- [DAQmxResetCIMemMapEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga300f32a4944c1f27b66baca7e78c78ab.html)

Parent topic:

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__general__properties__more__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga67a600b00ab1f21d4e51e2e90dd37aab.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__general__properties__more__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga67a600b00ab1f21d4e51e2e90dd37aab.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CI_DataXferReqCondRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the onboard memory of the device to the buffer.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_OnBrdMemMoreThanHalfFull10237Transfer data from the device when more than half of the onboard memory of

### DAQmx_CI_DataXferReqCond

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_DataXferReqCond

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the onboard memory of the device to the buffer. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_OnBrdMemMoreThanHalfFull | 10237 | Transfer data from the device when more than half of the onboard memory of the device fills. |
| DAQmx_Val_OnBrdMemNotEmpty | 10241 | Transfer data from the device when there is data in the onboard memory. |
| DAQmx_Val_OnbrdMemCustomThreshold | 12577 | Transfer data from the device when the number of samples specified with Data Transfer Custom Threshold are in the device FIFO. |
| DAQmx_Val_WhenAcqComplete | 12546 | Transfer data when the acquisition is complete. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIDataXferReqCond](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga7def264dabbee77c97109f13037ca616.html)
- [DAQmxSetCIDataXferReqCond](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gac80078394890c12aac567fbb37f5d46e.html)
- [DAQmxResetCIDataXferReqCond](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gad5273021b404303b6ab43ae0fb4185e8.html)

Data transfers take place independently from the application.DAQmx_Val_Interrupts10204Data transfers take place independently fr

### DAQmx_CI_DataXferMech

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_DataXferMech

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the data transfer mode for the channel. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_DMA | 10054 | Direct Memory Access. Data transfers take place independently from the application. |
| DAQmx_Val_Interrupts | 10204 | Data transfers take place independently from the application. Using interrupts increases CPU usage because the CPU must service interrupt requests. Typically, you should use interrupts if the device is out of DMA channels. |
| DAQmx_Val_ProgrammedIO | 10264 | Data transfers take place when you call an NI-DAQmx Read function or an NI-DAQmx Write function. |
| DAQmx_Val_USBbulk | 12590 | Data transfers take place independently from the application using a USB bulk pipe. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIDataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga250769f0d775ddf6bcddd7073c20800a.html)
- [DAQmxSetCIDataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gaca0d744564f29785a7f0912bcd75abe5.html)
- [DAQmxResetCIDataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga5dd75eccdb1461a92ec6eb36b5271423.html)

## TOPIC 01780: DAQmx_CI_Prescaler

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__general__properties__more__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1gac47c6acdd25ea7901dabd2af7002c707.html`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CI_PrescalerRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsuInt32Specifies the divisor to apply to the signal you connect to the counter source terminal. Scaled data that you read takes this setting into account. You should use a prescaler only when you connect an external signal to the counter

### DAQmx_CI_Prescaler

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_Prescaler

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| uInt32 | Specifies the divisor to apply to the signal you connect to the counter source terminal. Scaled data that you read takes this setting into account. You should use a prescaler only when you connect an external signal to the counter source terminal and when that signal has a higher frequency than the fastest onboard timebase. Setting this value disables duplicate count prevention unless you explicitly set Duplicate Count Prevention to TRUE. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIPrescaler](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga99dcde0a1d0b2f6176e2e627713607a3.html)
- [DAQmxSetCIPrescaler](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga93bb9fd5580f61b96005ebe900410d4a.html)
- [DAQmxResetCIPrescaler](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gabd309a9dc61831d29b0893ac954676b4.html)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CI_MaxMeasPeriodRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsfloat64Specifies the maximum period (in seconds) in which the device will recognize signals. For frequency measurements, a signal with a higher period than the one set in this property will return 0 Hz. For duty cycle, the device wil

### DAQmx_CI_MaxMeasPeriod

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_MaxMeasPeriod

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the maximum period (in seconds) in which the device will recognize signals. For frequency measurements, a signal with a higher period than the one set in this property will return 0 Hz. For duty cycle, the device will return 0 or 1 depending on the state of the line during the max defined period of time. Period measurements will return NaN. Pulse width measurement will return zero. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIMaxMeasPeriod](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga41ba64d6559e3ea3428b77a09308bb81.html)
- [DAQmxSetCIMaxMeasPeriod](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga0e229bb8744419597311605a3e48c080.html)
- [DAQmxResetCIMaxMeasPeriod](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gad1a2930d6dd3e28648abe73d547a9294.html)

Parent topic:

When Starting Edge is rising, the source signal must first fall below Threshold Level minus the hysteresis before a rising edge is detected at Threshold Level. When Start

### DAQmx_CI_Period_Hyst

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_Period_Hyst

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies a hysteresis level to apply to Threshold Level. When Starting Edge is rising, the source signal must first fall below Threshold Level minus the hysteresis before a rising edge is detected at Threshold Level. When Starting Edge is falling, the source signal must first rise above Threshold Level plus the hysteresis before a falling edge is detected at Threshold Level. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

### DAQmx_CI_Period_MeasTime

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_Period_MeasTime

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies in seconds the length of time to measure the period of the signal if Method is DAQmx_Val_HighFreq2Ctr. Measurement accuracy increases with increased measurement time and with increased signal frequency. If you measure a high-frequency signal for too long, however, the count register could roll over, which results in an incorrect measurement. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIPeriodMeasTime](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gaef94ca5bf1a27d9442a0a7366f682498.html)

## TOPIC 01818: DAQmx_CI_Encoder_DecodingType

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__position__linear__encoder_1gaa2a2ca44eecf5e75e2f8121e73bfcac7.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__position__linear__encoder_1gaa2a2ca44eecf5e75e2f8121e73bfcac7.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CI_Encoder_DecodingTypeRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies how to count and interpret the pulses the encoder generates on signal A and signal B. DAQmx_Val_X1, DAQmx_Val_X2, and DAQmx_Val_X4 are valid for quadrature encoders only. DAQmx_Val_TwoPulseCounting is valid for

### DAQmx_CI_Encoder_DecodingType

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_Encoder_DecodingType

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies how to count and interpret the pulses the encoder generates on signal A and signal B. DAQmx_Val_X1, DAQmx_Val_X2, and DAQmx_Val_X4 are valid for quadrature encoders only. DAQmx_Val_TwoPulseCounting is valid for two-pulse encoders only. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_X1 | 10090 | If signal A leads signal B, count the rising edges of signal A. If signal B leads signal A, count the falling edges of signal A. |
| DAQmx_Val_X2 | 10091 | Count the rising and falling edges of signal A. |
| DAQmx_Val_X4 | 10092 | Count the rising and falling edges of signal A and signal B. |
| DAQmx_Val_TwoPulseCounting | 10313 | Increment the count on rising edges of signal A. Decrement the count on rising edges of signal B. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIEncoderDecodingType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga845b9cb91332d6183fffd6565f6a9ed0.html)
- [DAQmxSetCIEncoderDecodingType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gab2f33714ce2e71ee757af97ad83b68c3.html)
- [DAQmxResetCIEncoderDecodingType](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga4fad254c96e466951cdca628606a9dfb.html)

Parent topic:

Linear Encoder

## TOPIC 01826: DAQmx_CI_Encoder_ZIndexPhase

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__position__z__input__digital__synchronization_1gaaba1506b12f3738e8085a9dcdedefc81.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__position__z__input__digital__synchronization_1gaaba1506b12f3738e8085a9dcdedefc81.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CI_Encoder_ZIndexPhaseRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the states at which signal A and signal B must be while signal Z is high for NI-DAQmx to reset the measurement. If signal Z is never high while signal A and signal B are high, for example, you must choose a phase

### DAQmx_CI_Encoder_ZIndexPhase

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_Encoder_ZIndexPhase

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the states at which signal A and signal B must be while signal Z is high for NI-DAQmx to reset the measurement. If signal Z is never high while signal A and signal B are high, for example, you must choose a phase other than DAQmx_Val_AHighBHigh. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_AHighBHigh | 10040 | Reset the measurement when signal A and signal B are high. |
| DAQmx_Val_AHighBLow | 10041 | Reset the measurement when signal A is high and signal B is low. |
| DAQmx_Val_ALowBHigh | 10042 | Reset the measurement when signal A is low and signal B high. |
| DAQmx_Val_ALowBLow | 10043 | Reset the measurement when signal A and signal B are low. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIEncoderZIndexPhase](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gaa23a273484908b356a295a339b17ea0c.html)
- [DAQmxSetCIEncoderZIndexPhase](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga561245e2b057e57f3cc0dbcf894873b8.html)
- [DAQmxResetCIEncoderZIndexPhase](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gac16ce91917329754448d8bdfd9f982f1.html)

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 01874: DAQmx_CI_GPS_SyncMethod

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__timestamp__gps_1ga304ef9523bd6841257c5bda7313c7a5e.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__input__timestamp__gps_1ga304ef9523bd6841257c5bda7313c7a5e.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CI_GPS_SyncMethodRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the method to use to synchronize the counter to a GPS receiver.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_IRIGB10070Use the IRIG-B synchronization method. The GPS receiver sends one synchronization pulse per second, as well as information

### DAQmx_CI_GPS_SyncMethod

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CI_GPS_SyncMethod

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the method to use to synchronize the counter to a GPS receiver. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_IRIGB | 10070 | Use the IRIG-B synchronization method. The GPS receiver sends one synchronization pulse per second, as well as information about the number of days, hours, minutes, and seconds that elapsed since the beginning of the current year. |
| DAQmx_Val_PPS | 10080 | Use the PPS synchronization method. The GPS receiver sends one synchronization pulse per second, but does not send any timing information. The timestamp measurement returns the number of seconds that elapsed since the device powered up unless you set Initial Seconds. |
| DAQmx_Val_None | 10230 | Do not synchronize the counter to a GPS receiver. The timestamp measurement returns the number of seconds that elapsed since the device powered up unless you set Initial Seconds. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCIGPSSyncMethod](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga43557b7b3dfc8ec1b1b25229b2006bf6.html)
- [DAQmxSetCIGPSSyncMethod](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gaa11a1f7393d6cbb8f0ce65a41e639424.html)
- [DAQmxResetCIGPSSyncMethod](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga90b815794c7e0f036054bf2857ece1a2.html)

Parent topic:

GPS

### DAQmx_CO_OutputType

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CO_OutputType

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Indicates how to define pulses generated on the channel. | Not Settable |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_Pulse_Time | 10269 | Generate pulses defined by the time the pulse is at a low state and the time the pulse is at a high state. |
| DAQmx_Val_Pulse_Freq | 10119 | Generate digital pulses defined by frequency and duty cycle. |
| DAQmx_Val_Pulse_Ticks | 10268 | Generate digital pulses defined by the number of timebase ticks that the pulse is at a low state and the number of timebase ticks that the pulse is at a high state. |

## TOPIC 01923: DAQmx_CO_CtrTimebaseMasterTimebaseDiv

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__output__general__properties__more_1ga9959b3a16b83bd944fd532c6b58ef49d.html`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CO_CtrTimebaseMasterTimebaseDivRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsuInt32Specifies the divisor for an external counter timebase. You can divide the counter timebase in order to generate slower signals without causing the count register to roll over.You can get/set/reset this property

### DAQmx_CO_CtrTimebaseMasterTimebaseDiv

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CO_CtrTimebaseMasterTimebaseDiv

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| uInt32 | Specifies the divisor for an external counter timebase. You can divide the counter timebase in order to generate slower signals without causing the count register to roll over. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

## TOPIC 01925: DAQmx_CO_MemMapEnable

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__output__general__properties__more__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga30366fa3fc05380c1f9fc93ac6196f4a.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__output__general__properties__more__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga30366fa3fc05380c1f9fc93ac6196f4a.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CO_MemMapEnableRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space

### DAQmx_CO_MemMapEnable

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CO_MemMapEnable

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCOMemMapEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga687798d50914410ca296c82cd88fb39e.html)
- [DAQmxSetCOMemMapEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gab4bb31034db3d7fc3409f40d44d92e9a.html)
- [DAQmxResetCOMemMapEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga5c068c03e8e02ee3ae2ad2922c78f68b.html)

Parent topic:

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__output__general__properties__more__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga543ede7127d0d2c662f97f80e39d350f.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__counter__output__general__properties__more__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga543ede7127d0d2c662f97f80e39d350f.html

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_CO_DataXferMechRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the data transfer mode for the device. For buffered operations, use DMA or USB Bulk. For non-buffered operations, use Polled.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_DMA10054Direct Memory Access. Data transfers take place independently fr

### DAQmx_CO_DataXferMech

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CO_DataXferMech

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the data transfer mode for the device. For buffered operations, use DMA or USB Bulk. For non-buffered operations, use Polled. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_DMA | 10054 | Direct Memory Access. Data transfers take place independently from the application. |
| DAQmx_Val_Interrupts | 10204 | Data transfers take place independently from the application. Using interrupts increases CPU usage because the CPU must service interrupt requests. Typically, you should use interrupts if the device is out of DMA channels. |
| DAQmx_Val_ProgrammedIO | 10264 | Data transfers take place when you call an NI-DAQmx Read function or an NI-DAQmx Write function. |
| DAQmx_Val_USBbulk | 12590 | Data transfers take place independently from the application using a USB bulk pipe. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetCODataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga523ef5dcd44b2e229f56f8a56331773f.html)
- [DAQmxSetCODataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gaea8c5a0f246f926920aecdcaf80de3d1.html)
- [DAQmxResetCODataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga73ee19ec197d7f646263c5b73057b734.html)

Parent topic:

### DAQmx_CO_DataXferReqCond

#### Syntax

DAQmx_CO_DataXferReqCond

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the buffer to the onboard memory of the device. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_OnBrdMemEmpty | 10235 | Transfer data to the device only when there is no data in the onboard memory of the device. |
| DAQmx_Val_OnBrdMemHalfFullOrLess | 10239 | Transfer data to the device any time the onboard memory is less than half full. |
| DAQmx_Val_OnBrdMemNotFull | 10242 | Transfer data to the device any time the onboard memory of the device is not full. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

## TOPIC 01943: DAQmx_DI_DigFltr_EnableBusMode

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__digital__input__digital__filter_1gab609f6ddae7eccc42f9adcee49d1b7e2.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__digital__input__digital__filter_1gab609f6ddae7eccc42f9adcee49d1b7e2.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_DI_DigFltr_EnableBusModeRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies whether to enable bus mode for digital filtering. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx treats all lines that use common filtering settings as a bus. If any line in the bus has jitter, all lines in the bu

### DAQmx_DI_DigFltr_EnableBusMode

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DI_DigFltr_EnableBusMode

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies whether to enable bus mode for digital filtering. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx treats all lines that use common filtering settings as a bus. If any line in the bus has jitter, all lines in the bus hold state until the entire bus stabilizes, or until 2 times the minimum pulse width elapses. If you set this property to FALSE, NI-DAQmx filters all lines individually. Jitter in one line does not affect other lines. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDIDigFltrEnableBusMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga7495ea990a77e8720b0be0e6c91fbfaf.html)
- [DAQmxSetDIDigFltrEnableBusMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga6c4508d340ef48b2e1365c48e9603a2f.html)
- [DAQmxResetDIDigFltrEnableBusMode](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gaacbaf6a4042386f6f1b32c19c4114dd9.html)

Parent topic:

A logic family corresponds to voltage thresholds that are compatible with a group of voltage standards. Refer to the device documentation for information on the logic high and log

### DAQmx_DI_LogicFamily

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DI_LogicFamily

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the logic family to use for acquisition. A logic family corresponds to voltage thresholds that are compatible with a group of voltage standards. Refer to the device documentation for information on the logic high and logic low voltages for these logic families. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_1point8V | 16184 | Compatible with 1.8 V CMOS signals. |
| DAQmx_Val_2point5V | 14620 | Compatible with 2.5 V CMOS signals. |
| DAQmx_Val_3point3V | 14621 | Compatible with LVTTL signals. |
| DAQmx_Val_5V | 14619 | Compatible with TTL and 5 V CMOS signals. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDILogicFamily](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gac30400d4fe524d76a994d87d88b2be52.html)
- [DAQmxSetDILogicFamily](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gaf497c8a52f5cf3b3f2ab3bdb0c17574b.html)
- [DAQmxResetDILogicFamily](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gaa352a7712cb52d36ac2648d996ae2b2f.html)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`

- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_DI_TristateRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies whether to tristate the lines in the channel. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx tristates the lines in the channel. If you set this property to FALSE, NI-DAQmx does not modify the configuration of the lines even i

### DAQmx_DI_Tristate

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DI_Tristate

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies whether to tristate the lines in the channel. If you set this property to TRUE, NI-DAQmx tristates the lines in the channel. If you set this property to FALSE, NI-DAQmx does not modify the configuration of the lines even if the lines were previously tristated. Set this property to FALSE to read lines in other tasks or to read output-only lines. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDITristate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gacbdd124d1754d63501dd86a32d3d4103.html)
- [DAQmxSetDITristate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gaafec7ef0cd2781c48a796e5a090d3da3.html)
- [DAQmxResetDITristate](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gad7b80892f7b4e9f437aafbd67f4912d4.html)

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 01951: DAQmx_DI_DataXferReqCond

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__digital__input__general__properties__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga3878feb68732f59f42ffbc92aced5660.html`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_DI_DataXferReqCondRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the onboard memory of the device to the buffer.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_OnBrdMemMoreThanHalfFull10237Transfer data from the device when more than half of the onboard memory of

### DAQmx_DI_DataXferReqCond

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DI_DataXferReqCond

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies under what condition to transfer data from the onboard memory of the device to the buffer. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_OnBrdMemMoreThanHalfFull | 10237 | Transfer data from the device when more than half of the onboard memory of the device fills. |
| DAQmx_Val_OnBrdMemNotEmpty | 10241 | Transfer data from the device when there is data in the onboard memory. |
| DAQmx_Val_OnbrdMemCustomThreshold | 12577 | Transfer data from the device when the number of samples specified with Data Transfer Custom Threshold are in the device FIFO. |
| DAQmx_Val_WhenAcqComplete | 12546 | Transfer data when the acquisition is complete. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDIDataXferReqCond](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gaa962ead9f95fbc11a4a876b30ba0d3d3.html)
- [DAQmxSetDIDataXferReqCond](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gaaf1d5f56f1ae4491f277252e066fc537.html)
- [DAQmxResetDIDataXferReqCond](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gae9c3c9cb161c76cd0b31e5890a4f2866.html)

## TOPIC 01953: DAQmx_DI_DataXferMech

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__digital__input__general__properties__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga7e0065f623418dd7f8e800c2071bb5f7.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__digital__input__general__properties__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga7e0065f623418dd7f8e800c2071bb5f7.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_DI_DataXferMechRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the data transfer mode for the device.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_DMA10054Direct Memory Access. Data transfers take place independently from the application.DAQmx_Val_Interrupts10204Data transfers take place independently fro

### DAQmx_DI_DataXferMech

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DI_DataXferMech

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the data transfer mode for the device. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_DMA | 10054 | Direct Memory Access. Data transfers take place independently from the application. |
| DAQmx_Val_Interrupts | 10204 | Data transfers take place independently from the application. Using interrupts increases CPU usage because the CPU must service interrupt requests. Typically, you should use interrupts if the device is out of DMA channels. |
| DAQmx_Val_ProgrammedIO | 10264 | Data transfers take place when you call an NI-DAQmx Read function or an NI-DAQmx Write function. |
| DAQmx_Val_USBbulk | 12590 | Data transfers take place independently from the application using a USB bulk pipe. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDIDataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gaec76b13e0c348d9c6bbbb57253f3965a.html)
- [DAQmxSetDIDataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1ga2b558f66c703b1d240c408d1c4975c8b.html)
- [DAQmxResetDIDataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga551e35689b2f760c999748d41b358786.html)

## TOPIC 01955: DAQmx_DI_MemMapEnable

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__digital__input__general__properties__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1gaec1d0ff430666be738f8f3d55e25e903.html`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_DI_MemMapEnableRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsbool32Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space

### DAQmx_DI_MemMapEnable

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DI_MemMapEnable

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| bool32 | Specifies for NI-DAQmx to map hardware registers to the memory space of the application, if possible. Normally, NI-DAQmx maps hardware registers to memory accessible only to the kernel. Mapping the registers to the memory space of the application increases performance. However, if the application accesses the memory space mapped to the registers, it can adversely affect the operation of the device and possibly result in a system crash. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDIMemMapEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga804953b7f465274ce8e52258e087790a.html)
- [DAQmxSetDIMemMapEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gae669d2084f23b7719b15770462820c2a.html)
- [DAQmxResetDIMemMapEnable](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga99fe8216ccfcf88b5b74a17bcafec683.html)

Parent topic:

### DAQmx_DO_OutputDriveType

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DO_OutputDriveType

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the drive type for digital output channels. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_ActiveDrive | 12573 | Drive the output pin to approximately 0 V for logic low and +3.3 V or +5 V, depending on the device, for logic high. |
| DAQmx_Val_OpenCollector | 12574 | Drive the output pin to 0 V for logic low. For logic high, the output driver assumes a high-impedance state and does not drive a voltage. |

## TOPIC 01965: DAQmx_DO_DataXferMech

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__digital__output__general__properties__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga612025656af2596aae06f0006da876e0.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__channel__digital__output__general__properties__advanced__data__transfer__and__memory_1ga612025656af2596aae06f0006da876e0.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_DO_DataXferMechRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the data transfer mode for the device.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_DMA10054Direct Memory Access. Data transfers take place independently from the application.DAQmx_Val_Interrupts10204Data transfers take place independently fro

### DAQmx_DO_DataXferMech

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DO_DataXferMech

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the data transfer mode for the device. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_DMA | 10054 | Direct Memory Access. Data transfers take place independently from the application. |
| DAQmx_Val_Interrupts | 10204 | Data transfers take place independently from the application. Using interrupts increases CPU usage because the CPU must service interrupt requests. Typically, you should use interrupts if the device is out of DMA channels. |
| DAQmx_Val_ProgrammedIO | 10264 | Data transfers take place when you call an NI-DAQmx Read function or an NI-DAQmx Write function. |
| DAQmx_Val_USBbulk | 12590 | Data transfers take place independently from the application using a USB bulk pipe. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDODataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga0e22e6898c6a51d6c7a27a7f662ce208.html)
- [DAQmxSetDODataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gad637df36122801de4c08a72143b1d89b.html)
- [DAQmxResetDODataXferMech](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga025eb206549356e486b63c063115b63d.html)

- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_DO_LineStates_PausedStateRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Specifies the state of the lines in a digital output task when the task pauses.Valid valuesDAQmx_Val_High10192Logic high.DAQmx_Val_Low10214Logic low.DAQmx_Val_Tristate10310High-impedance state. You can select this state

### DAQmx_DO_LineStates_PausedState

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DO_LineStates_PausedState

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies the state of the lines in a digital output task when the task pauses. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_High | 10192 | Logic high. |
| DAQmx_Val_Low | 10214 | Logic low. |
| DAQmx_Val_Tristate | 10310 | High-impedance state. You can select this state only on devices with bidirectional lines. You cannot select this state for dedicated digital output lines. On some devices, you can select this value only for entire ports. |
| DAQmx_Val_NoChange | 10160 | Do not change the state of the lines. On some devices, you can select this value only for entire ports. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDOLineStatesPausedState](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gac47f8a235633206ae40b19acab5ea2c6.html)
- [DAQmxSetDOLineStatesPausedState](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__setter_1gaf0070e064514ec35b34888649e2e7bb7.html)
- [DAQmxResetDOLineStatesPausedState](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1gab2e54187312d948cf1de0a1c248705af.html)

### DAQmx_DO_Overcurrent_Limit

#### Syntax

DAQmx_DO_Overcurrent_Limit

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| float64 | Specifies the current threshold in Amperes for the channel. A value of 0 means the channel observes no limit. Devices can monitor only a finite number of current thresholds simultaneously. If you attempt to monitor additional thresholds, NI-DAQmx returns an error. |  |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_Pwr_OutputStateRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32Indicates power channel operating state. Can be read at any time during a task.Not SettableValid valuesDAQmx_Val_ConstantVoltage15500Power output is maintaining a constant voltage by adjusting the current.DAQmx_Val_ConstantCurren

### DAQmx_Pwr_OutputState

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Pwr_OutputState

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Indicates power channel operating state. Can be read at any time during a task. | Not Settable |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_ConstantVoltage | 15500 | Power output is maintaining a constant voltage by adjusting the current. |
| DAQmx_Val_ConstantCurrent | 15501 | Power output is maintaining a constant current by adjusting the voltage. |
| DAQmx_Val_Overvoltage | 15502 | Voltage output has exceeded its limit. |
| DAQmx_Val_OutputDisabled | 15503 | Power output is disabled. |

You can get this property using:

- [DAQmxGetPwrOutputState](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gaf636aee9a42cb881e403123abacaa73c.html)

Parent topic:

### DAQmx_Pwr_RemoteSense

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Pwr_RemoteSense

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Specifies whether to use local or remote sense to sense the output voltage. DAQmx Read (Power Supply) will return remote or local voltage based on the Remote Sense attribute value. Reading this property will return the user-defined value. |  |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_Local | 16095 | Local. |
| DAQmx_Val_Remote | 16096 | Remote. |

You can get/set/reset this property using:

- [DAQmxGetPwrRemoteSense](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga6bb839f4c1f562d17a6f65d7c8783b5d.html)

- [DAQmxResetPwrRemoteSense](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__resetter_1ga8a02ad97ea5d246618dea14468fc7864.html)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_Dev_AO_SampModesRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32*Indicates sample modes supported by devices that support sample clocked analog output.Not SettableValid valuesDAQmx_Val_FiniteSamps10178Acquire or generate a finite number of samples.DAQmx_Val_ContSamps10123Acquire or generate

### DAQmx_Dev_AO_SampModes

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Dev_AO_SampModes

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32* | Indicates sample modes supported by devices that support sample clocked analog output. | Not Settable |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_FiniteSamps | 10178 | Acquire or generate a finite number of samples. |
| DAQmx_Val_ContSamps | 10123 | Acquire or generate samples until you stop the task. |
| DAQmx_Val_HWTimedSinglePoint | 12522 | Acquire or generate samples continuously using hardware timing without a buffer. Hardware timed single point sample mode is supported only for the sample clock and change detection timing types. |

You can get this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDevAOSampModes](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1gaa3ad9106fa533340896bb332f3c6e766.html)

DAQmx_Dev_AO_TrigUsage

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32 | Indicates the triggers supported by this device for analog output tasks. | Not Settable |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| DAQmx_Val_Bit_TriggerUsageTypes_Pause | 2 | Device supports pause triggers |
| DAQmx_Val_Bit_TriggerUsageTypes_Reference | 4 | Device supports reference triggers |
| DAQmx_Val_Bit_TriggerUsageTypes_Start | 8 | Device supports start triggers |
| DAQmx_Val_Bit_TriggerUsageTypes_Handshake | 16 | Device supports handshake triggers |
| DAQmx_Val_Bit_TriggerUsageTypes_ArmStart | 32 | Device supports arm start triggers |

## TOPIC 01997: DAQmx_Dev_CI_SupportedMeasTypes

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__device__i__o__type__counter__input_1gaac3b6c2d914c389b612ba7198431943e.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group__ni-daqmx__c__properties__device__i__o__type__counter__input_1gaac3b6c2d914c389b612ba7198431943e.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: SyntaxDAQmx_Dev_CI_SupportedMeasTypesRemarksData TypeDescriptionRestrictionsint32*Indicates the measurement types supported by the physical channels of the device. Refer to Measurement Types for information on specific channels.Not SettableValid valuesDAQmx_Val_CountEdges10125Count edges of a digita

### DAQmx_Dev_CI_SupportedMeasTypes

#### Syntax

DAQmx_Dev_CI_SupportedMeasTypes

#### Remarks

| Data Type | Description | Restrictions |
| --- | --- | --- |
| int32* | Indicates the measurement types supported by the physical channels of the device. Refer to Measurement Types for information on specific channels. | Not Settable |

| Valid values |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| DAQmx_Val_CountEdges | 10125 | Count edges of a digital signal. |
| DAQmx_Val_Freq | 10179 | Measure the frequency of a digital signal. |
| DAQmx_Val_Period | 10256 | Measure the period of a digital signal. |
| DAQmx_Val_PulseWidth | 10359 | Measure the width of a pulse of a digital signal. |
| DAQmx_Val_SemiPeriod | 10289 | Measure the time between state transitions of a digital signal. |
| DAQmx_Val_PulseFrequency | 15864 | Pulse measurement, returning the result as frequency and duty cycle. |
| DAQmx_Val_PulseTime | 15865 | Pulse measurement, returning the result as high time and low time. |
| DAQmx_Val_PulseTicks | 15866 | Pulse measurement, returning the result as high ticks and low ticks. |
| DAQmx_Val_DutyCycle | 16070 | Measure the duty cycle of a digital signal. |
| DAQmx_Val_Position_AngEncoder | 10360 | Angular position measurement using an angular encoder. |
| DAQmx_Val_Position_LinEncoder | 10361 | Linear position measurement using a linear encoder. |
| DAQmx_Val_Velocity_AngEncoder | 16078 | Angular velocity measurement using an angular encoder. |
| DAQmx_Val_Velocity_LinEncoder | 16079 | Linear velocity measurement using a linear encoder. |
| DAQmx_Val_TwoEdgeSep | 10267 | Measure time between edges of two digital signals. |
| DAQmx_Val_GPS_Timestamp | 10362 | Timestamp measurement, synchronizing the counter to a GPS receiver. |

You can get this property using:

- [DAQmxGetDevCISupportedMeasTypes](group__ni-daqmx__c__functions__property__manipulation__getter_1ga6e10b3055050ca6f387ecaab3ff8c2f7.html)

Parent topic:
